<script type="text/javascript">
    (function(){
        var nav = document.getElementById('Jheader');
        var li= nav.getElementsByTagName('li');
        for (var i = li.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
            li[i].onmouseover=function(){
                var cn=this.className;
                this.className=cn+" on";
            }
            li[i].onmouseout=function(){
                var cn=this.className;
                this.className=cn.replace(" on","");
            }
        };

        //车友app下载控制
        var appLoad=document.getElementById("header_app_load").getElementsByTagName("a")[0];
        var appEwm=document.getElementById("header_app_load").getElementsByTagName("p")[0];
        appLoad.onmouseover=function (){this.className+=" hov";appEwm.style.display="block";}
        appLoad.onmouseout=function (){this.className=this.className.replace(" hov","");appEwm.style.display="none";}
    })();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	//去其他论坛
	function showViewOtherForum() {
		showWin=dhtmlmodal.open('showFlow', 'iframe', '//www.pcauto.com.cn/forum/1403/intf3167.html', '', 'width=780px,height=450px,center=1,resize=0,scrolling=0', "recal");
		document.getElementById('showFlow').firstChild.getElementsByTagName('a')[0].onclick = function () {
			document.getElementById('showFlow').style.display = 'none';
			document.getElementById('interVeil').style.display = 'none';
		}
		return false;
	
	}
</script>

    function jiankong(chanalId){
        var img=document.createElement("img");
        var TagId=chanalId;
        img.src="//count.pcauto.com.cn/count.php?channel="+TagId+"&screen="+screen.width+"*"+screen.height+"&refer="+encodeURIComponent(document.referrer)+"&anticache="+new Date().getTime()+"&url="+encodeURIComponent(location.href)+"&from=event";
    }

        jiankong(671);    
    }

    //切换是否新窗打开帖子
    function switchTopicOpenMode(){
        var mode = $("#topicOpenMode:checked").length === 1;
        if(mode){
            $("a.topicurl").attr("target", "_blank");
            $.cookie("dontOpenTopicInNewWindow", 0, { expires: 100});
        }else{
            jiankong(672);
            $("a.topicurl").removeAttr("target");
            $.cookie("dontOpenTopicInNewWindow", 1, { expires: 100});
        }
    }
    //读是否新窗打开帖子的cookie
    if($.cookie("dontOpenTopicInNewWindow") === "1"){
        $("#topicOpenMode").removeAttr("checked");
        $("a.topicurl").removeAttr("target");
    }

    var visitedfid = $.cookie("visitedfid");
    if (visitedfid == null || visitedfid == '') {
        visitedfid = '17442';
    } else {
        var fids = visitedfid.split('D');
        for (var i = 0; i < fids.length; i++) {
            if(fids[i] == '17442') {
                fids.splice(i, 1); break;
            }
        }
        fids.unshift('17442');
        if (fids.length > 10) fids.pop()
        visitedfid = fids.join("D");
    }
    $.cookie('visitedfid', null);
    $.cookie('visitedfid', visitedfid, { expires: 100, domain: 'pcauto.com.cn'});

    //fix条用户登录信息提醒功能
    var fixlogin_showtip = false;
    var fixlogin_timer = null;
    var fixlogin_msgtotal = 0;
    //相关方法移到异步加载js里

    function resizeImg(maxWidth,maxHeight,objImg){
        var img = new Image();
        img.src = objImg.src;
        var hRatio;
        var wRatio;
        var Ratio = 1;
        var w = img.width;
        var h = img.height;
        wRatio = maxWidth / w;
        hRatio = maxHeight / h;
        if (maxWidth ==0 && maxHeight==0){
            Ratio = 1;
        }else if (maxWidth==0){//
            if (hRatio<1) Ratio = hRatio;
        }else if (maxHeight==0){
            if (wRatio<1) Ratio = wRatio;
        }else if (wRatio<1 || hRatio<1){
            Ratio = (wRatio<=hRatio?wRatio:hRatio);
        }
        if (Ratio<1){
            w = w * Ratio;
            h = h * Ratio;
        }
        objImg.height = h;
        objImg.width = w;
    }
    (function() {
        var img = document.getElementById('logoImg');
        if(!!img){
            var src2 = img.getAttribute('src2');
            img.onload = function(){
                resizeImg(120,90,img);
            };
            img.setAttribute('src',src2);
        }
    })();

</script>


<script >
    function goPost(id,callback){
        addCount(id);
        if(callback){
            callback();
        }
    }
    function goPostByUrl(id,url,flag){
        addCount(id);
        if(url){
        	if(flag){
        		window.open(url);
        	}else{
        		  location.href=url;
        	}
          
        }
    }
    function addCount(id){
         tagid=id;
        var img = new Image();
        img.src="//count.pcauto.com.cn/count.php?channel="+tagid+"&screen="+screen.width+"*"+screen.height+"&refer="+encodeURIComponent(document.referrer)
                +"&anticache="+new Date().getTime()+"&url="+encodeURIComponent(location.href)+"&from=event";
    }
    function goCreateTopic(url,flag){
        goPostByUrl("195",url,flag);
    }
</script>

                <script>
                    function ivyLoadReal(closespan){
                        var ad=null, adpos=document.getElementsByTagName("u");
                        for(var i=0; i<adpos.length; i++) if(adpos[i].className=="adpos"){ ad=adpos[i]; break; }
                        if(ad==null) return;
                        if(!closespan) {
                            document.write("<span id=adpos_"+ad.id+" style=display:none>");
                            showIvyViaJs(ad.id);
                            return;
                        }
                        document.write("</span>");
                        var real=document.getElementById("adpos_"+ad.id);
                        for(var i=0; i<real.childNodes.length; i++) {
                            var node=real.childNodes[i];
                            if(node.tagName=="SCRIPT" && /closespan/.test(node.className)) continue;
                            ad.parentNode.insertBefore(node,ad); i--
                        }
                        ad.parentNode.removeChild(ad);
                        real.parentNode.removeChild(real);
                    }
                </script>

<script>
function add_tab(){
    var _target= $('#add_tab_0302 .add_tab_0302_con');
    var _control=$('#add_tab_0302 .add_tab_0302_ctrl .cur');
    var _submark=$("#add_tab_0302 .add_tab_0302_ctrl .submark");
    _target.hide();
    _target.eq(0).show();
    _control.eq(0).addClass("current");
    _submark.eq(0).show();
    _control.mouseover(function(){
        var _index=$(this).index();
        _target.hide();
        _target.eq(_index).show();
        _control.removeClass("current");
        _control.eq(_index).addClass("current");
        _submark.hide();
        _submark.eq(_index).show();

    })
}
add_tab()
</script>
<!--切换车问答欲专栏导航end-->

            $(document).ready(function () {
                if (typeof newsArray !== "undefined"){

                }

                //setFixBox();
                    if (!$("#subjectClass>a").hasClass('current')){
                        $("#subjectClass").hover(function(){
                            $("#subjectClass_con").show();
                            $("#subjectClass>a").addClass("focus");
                        },function(){
                            $("#subjectClass_con").hide();
                            $("#subjectClass>a").removeClass("focus");

                function setCMS(data){
                    var dlength = data.length;
                    for (var i = 0, length = 0;i < length;i++){
                        if(i%2 == 0){
                            var id = Math.floor(Math.random() * dlength);
                            var obj = data[id];
                            $("#middle_ad_" + i).html(obj);
                        }
                    }
                }

                //帖子类型导航栏
                function setFixBox() {
                    var fixbox = $("#category"),
                    list_con = $("#topic_list")[0]?$("#topic_list"):$("#picture_post_list")
                    fixBoxTop=fixbox.offset().top,
                    maxTop=list_con.offset().top+list_con.height();
                    var fixbox_place = function(){
                        var sTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop;
                        if(document.attachEvent && window.ActiveXObject && !window.XMLHttpRequest){//ie6
                            if (sTop>fixBoxTop && sTop<maxTop) {
                                fixbox.removeClass('relative').addClass('absolute').css("top",sTop);
                            }else{
                                fixbox.removeClass('absolute').css("top",0).addClass('relative');
                            }
                        } else if (sTop>fixBoxTop && sTop<maxTop) {
                            fixbox.removeClass('relative').addClass('fixed fixed-top');
                        } else {
                            fixbox.removeClass('fixed fixed-top').addClass('relative');
                        }
                    }
                    $(window).bind("scroll",function(){
                        fixbox_place();
                    });
                    $(window).bind("load",function(){
                        fixbox_place();
                    });
                }

                function Down(targets,controls){
                    this.targets = targets,
                    this.controls = controls
                    this.init();
                }
                Down.prototype={
                    init:function(){
                        var _this=this
                        _this.controls.mousemove(function(){_this.targets.show();});
                        _this.targets.mouseleave(function(){_this.targets.hide();} );
                    }
                }
                new Down($("#dIguest"), $("#dIguest_more"));

                            function fixlogin_msgtip(ncount,rcount,mcount,total,cmtcount){
                                var msgtip = $("#fixloginbox .msgtip");
                                var tipHtml = '<i class="close" id="fixlogin_closetip"></i>';
                                if(ncount>0){
                                    tipHtml += '<p id="fixbox_noticelink"><span>'+ncount+'</span> 个系统通知，<a onclick="fixlogin_closemsg(this,\'t1\','+ncount+')" href="//my.pcauto.com.cn/msg/notice.jsp" target="_blank">查看通知</a></p>';
                                }
                                if(rcount>0){
                                    tipHtml += '<p id="fixbox_replylink"><span>'+rcount+'</span> 个论坛回复，<a onclick="fixlogin_closemsg(this,\'t2\','+rcount+')" href="//my.pcauto.com.cn/forum/receivereply.jsp" target="_blank">查看回复</a></p>';
                                }
                                if(cmtcount>0){
                                    tipHtml += '<p id="fixbox_cmtlink"><span>'+cmtcount+'</span> 个评论回复，<a onclick="fixlogin_closemsg(this,\'t4\','+cmtcount+')" href="//my.pcauto.com.cn/cmt/receivereply.jsp" target="_blank">查看回复</a></p>';
                                }
                                if(mcount>0){
                                    tipHtml += '<p id="fixbox_messagelink"><span>'+mcount+'</span> 条私信，<a onclick="fixlogin_closemsg(this,\'t3\','+mcount+')" href="//my.pcauto.com.cn/msg/inbox.jsp?pageNo=1" target="_blank">查看私信</a></p>';
                                }
                                msgtip.html(tipHtml);
                                msgtip.show();
                                $.cookie("show_msgtip", "yes", {expires: 10});
                                $.cookie("msg_count", total, {expires: 10});
                                fixlogin_showtip=true;
                                $("#fixlogin_closetip").click(function(){
                                    msgtip.hide();
                                    $.cookie("show_msgtip", "no", {expires: 10});
                                    fixlogin_showtip=false;
                                })
                            };


                            function fixlogin_closemsg(obj,msgtypename,msgcounts){
                                var msgcount = $("#fixloginbox .msgtip p").length;
                                if(msgcount == 1){
                                    $("#fixloginbox .msgtip").hide();
                                    fixlogin_showtip = false;
                                    $("#fixloginbox .msg").removeClass("news");
                                    $("#fixloginbox .msgname em").hide();
                                    $("#msgtip").hide();
                                    f_Logan.showtip = false;
                                    $("#msg").removeClass("news");
                                    $("#msgname em").hide();
                                }else{
                                    $(obj).parent().remove();
                                    if(msgtypename=="t1"){
                                        $("#noticemsg").remove();
                                    }else if(msgtypename=="t2"){
                                        $("#replymsg").remove();
                                    }else if(msgtypename=="t3"){
                                        $("#messagemsg").remove();
                                    }else if(msgtypename=="t4"){
                                        $("#cmtmsg").remove();
                                    }
                                    var newmsgcount = fixlogin_msgtotal - msgcounts;
                                    if(newmsgcount.toString().length>3){
                                        $("#fixloginbox .msgname em").html("999");
                                        $("#msgname em").html("999");
                                    }else{
                                        $("#fixloginbox .msgname em").html(newmsgcount);
                                        $("#msgname em").html(newmsgcount);
                                    }
                                }
                                $("#fixloginbox ."+msgtypename).find("em").hide();
                                var msgtypelinkid;
                                if(msgtypename=="t1"){
                                    msgtypelinkid="noticelink";
                                }else if(msgtypename=="t2"){
                                    msgtypelinkid="replylink";
                                }else if(msgtypename=="t3"){
                                    msgtypelinkid="messagelink";
                                }else if(msgtypename=="t4"){
                                    msgtypelinkid="cmtlink";
                                }
                                $("#"+msgtypelinkid).find("em").hide();
                            }

                            $.getJSON("//bip.pcauto.com.cn/intf/message.jsp?act=getNumToJson&siteId=2&status=0&callback=?",function(data){
                                var total = 0;
                                var msg = $("#fixloginbox .msg");
                                var msgname = $("#fixloginbox .msgname");
                                total = data.messageCount + data.systemNoticeCount + data.forumReplyCount + data.commentReplyCount;
                                fixlogin_msgtotal = total;
                                if(total>0){
                                    msg.addClass("news");
                                    if(total.toString().length>3){
                                        msgname.html(msgname.html()+'<em>999</em>');
                                    }else{
                                        msgname.html(msgname.html()+'<em>'+total+'</em>');
                                    }

                                    if(data.systemNoticeCount>0){
                                        if(data.systemNoticeCount.toString().length>3){
                                            $("#fixloginbox .t1").html($("#fixloginbox .t1").html()+'<em>999</em>');
                                        }else{
                                            $("#fixloginbox .t1").html($("#fixloginbox .t1").html()+'<em>'+data.systemNoticeCount+'</em>');
                                        }
                                    }
                                    if(data.commentReplyCount>0){
                                        if(data.commentReplyCount.toString().length>3){
                                            $("#fixloginbox .t4").html($("#fixloginbox .t4").html()+'<em>999</em>');
                                        }else{
                                            $("#fixloginbox .t4").html($("#fixloginbox .t4").html()+'<em>'+data.commentReplyCount+'</em>');
                                        }
                                    }
                                    if(data.forumReplyCount>0){
                                        $("#fixloginbox .msgname a").attr("href","//my.pcauto.com.cn/forum/receivereply.jsp");
                                        if(data.forumReplyCount.toString().length>3){
                                            $("#fixloginbox .t2").html($("#fixloginbox .t2").html()+'<em>999</em>');
                                        }else{
                                            $("#fixloginbox .t2").html($("#fixloginbox .t2").html()+'<em>'+data.forumReplyCount+'</em>');
                                        }
                                    }
                                    if(data.messageCount>0){
                                        if(data.messageCount.toString().length>3){
                                            $("#fixloginbox .t3").html($("#fixloginbox .t3").html()+'<em>999</em>');
                                        }else{
                                            $("#fixloginbox .t3").html($("#fixloginbox .t3").html()+'<em>'+data.messageCount+'</em>');
                                        }
                                    }
                                    if($.cookie("show_msgtip") && $.cookie("msg_count")){
                                        var show_msgtip_state = $.cookie("show_msgtip");
                                        var msg_count_cookie = $.cookie("msg_count");
                                        if(show_msgtip_state=="no" && msg_count_cookie==total){
                                            return;
                                        }else{
                                            fixlogin_msgtip(data.systemNoticeCount,data.forumReplyCount,data.messageCount,total,data.commentReplyCount);
                                        }
                                    }else{
                                        fixlogin_msgtip(data.systemNoticeCount,data.forumReplyCount,data.messageCount,total,data.commentReplyCount);
                                    }
                                }
                            })

                                if(!this.getElementsByTagName("em")[0]){
                                    return;
                                }
                                var msgcount = this.getElementsByTagName("em")[0].innerHTML;
                                var linktypeclass = this.className;
                                var msgtypename;
                                if(linktypeclass == "t1"){
                                    msgtypename=document.getElementById("fixbox_noticelink").getElementsByTagName("a")[0];
                                }else if(linktypeclass == "t2"){
                                    msgtypename=document.getElementById("fixbox_replylink").getElementsByTagName("a")[0];
                                }else if(linktypeclass == "t3"){
                                    msgtypename=document.getElementById("fixbox_messagelink").getElementsByTagName("a")[0];
                                }else if(linktypeclass == "t4"){
                                    //6-16
                                    msgtypename=document.getElementById("fixbox_cmtlink").getElementsByTagName("a")[0];
                                }
                                fixlogin_closemsg(msgtypename,linktypeclass,msgcount);
                            });

        <script type="text/javascript">
            function Cdown(targets,controls,callback){
                this.targets = targets,
                this.controls = controls,
                this.callback = callback ? callback:function(){};
                this.init();
            }
            Cdown.prototype={
                init:function(){
                    var _this=this;
                    _this.controls.click(function(){
                        _this.targets.show();
                        _this.callback();
                    });
                    _this.controls.mouseleave(function(){
                        _this.targets.hide();
                        _this.callback();
                    });
                }
            }
            new Cdown($("#timeScroll_con"),$("#timeScroll"));
            new Cdown($("#paixu_con"),$("#paixu"));

            var showMsgObj = $("#showMsg");
            function showMessage(message){
                if(jQuery.browser.msie6){
                    alert(message);
                }else{
                    showMsgObj.html(showErrorMsg.replace('[:MSG]',message));
                    setTimeout(function(){tb_show_2('','#TB_inline?inlineId=showMsg&width=340',false);},50);
                }
            }

            //发贴按钮
            var post_btn_top = $(".btn_top").find("ul");
            $(".btn_top").hover(function(){
                post_btn_top.show();
            },function(){
                setTimeout(function(){ post_btn_top.hide();
                },250);
            });
            var post_btn_bottom = $(".btn_bottom").find("ul");
            $(".btn_bottom").hover(function(){
                post_btn_bottom.show();
            },function(){
                setTimeout(function(){ post_btn_bottom.hide();
                },250);
            });

            modclickcount = 0;
            //增加浮动效果
            // ---start---
            var tips = document.getElementById('admin-layer');
            var pos;
            var scroll = 0;
            var differ = 0;
            window.onscroll=function(){
                if (window.innerHeight) {
                    pos = window.pageYOffset
                }
                else if (document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollTop) {
                    pos = document.documentElement.scrollTop
                }
                else if (document.body) {
                    pos = document.body.scrollTop;
                }
                differ = pos - scroll;
                if(pos ==  differ)
                {
                    scroll = pos;
                    differ = 0;
                }
                else {
                    scroll = pos;
                }
                if(modclickcount!=0)document.getElementById("admin-layer").style.top=parseInt(tips.offsetTop + differ) + "px";
            };
            //  ---end---

            function modclick(obj) {
                if(obj.checked) {
                    modclickcount++;
                    if(modclickcount == 1){
                        addTid(obj.value);
                    }else{
                        cleanTid();
                    }
                } else {
                    modclickcount--;
                    cleanTid();
                    if(modclickcount == 1){
                        $("input[name='moderate[]']:checked").each(function(){
                            addTid(this.value);
                        });
                    }
                }
                $('#modcount').html(modclickcount);
                $('.admlink').attr("title","选中" + modclickcount+ "篇");
                if(modclickcount > 0) {
                    var top_offset = obj.offsetTop;
                    while((obj = obj.offsetParent).id != 'topic_list') {
                        top_offset += obj.offsetTop;
                    }
                    $('#admin-layer').css("top", top_offset - 11);
                    $('#admin-layer').show();
                } else {
                    $('#admin-layer').hide();
                }
            }

            //清除admlink后面的tid参数
            function cleanTid(){
                $(".admlink").each(function(){
                    var thisHref = $(this).attr("href");
                    if(thisHref.indexOf("&tid=") > 0){
                        $(this).attr("href", thisHref.replace(/&tid=\d+/g,""));
                    }
                });
            }
            //添加admlink后面的tid参数
            function addTid(id){
                $(".admlink").each(function(){
                    $(this).attr("href",$(this).attr("href") + "&tid=" + id);
                });
            }
            function checkall(form, prefix, checkall) {
                var checkall = checkall ? checkall : 'chkall';
                count = 0;
                for(var i = 0; i < form.elements.length; i++) {
                    var e = form.elements[i];
                    if(e.name && e.name != checkall && (!prefix || (prefix && e.name.match(prefix)))) {
                        e.checked = form.elements[checkall].checked;
                        if(e.checked) {
                            count++;
                        }
                    }
                }
                $('.admlink').attr("title","" + count+ "");
                return count;
            }
            //在线用户套橙色
            var DisplayOnline = (function () {
                var my = {};
                var unique = function(s){
                    if (!s && typeof s !== 'Array') return [];
                    var newArray=[];
                    var temp = {};
                    var item = {};
                    for (var i = 0 ; (item= s[i]) != null; i++) {
                        if (!temp[item]) {
                            newArray.push(item);
                            temp[item] = true;
                        }
                    }
                    return newArray;
                }
                my.run = function () {
                    var onlineIds = [];
                    var re = /user-([\d]+).*/ig;
                    $('.needonline').each(function() {
                        onlineIds.push(this.className.replace(re,'$1'));
                    });
                }

                return my ;
            }());
            DisplayOnline.run();

                if (jQuery.browser.msie6) {
                    tips = "您还没有登录,请先登录";
                }
                showMessage(tips);
            }

                    a.html("<img alt=\"收藏此版块\" src=\"//www1.pcauto.com.cn/bbs/2014/images/addfav.png\">");
                }
            }

                    getCarHtml:function(item){
                        var html = "";
                        switch(item.type){
                            case 0:
                                html=this.getSupperBuyCarHtml(item);
                                break;
                            case 1:
                                html=this.getBuyCarTicketHtml(item);
                                break;
                            case 2:
                                html=this.getGroupBuyHtml(item);
                                break;
                            case 3:
                                html=this.getMallCarHtml(item);
                                break;
                            default:
                                break;
                        }
                        return html;
                    },

                    replceSrc :function(target, type) {
                        if(target && target.getElementsByTagName("img")){
                            var imgs = target.getElementsByTagName("img");
                            for (var i = 0,len = imgs.length; i < len; i++) {
                                if (imgs[i].getAttribute(type)) {
                                    imgs[i].src = imgs[i].getAttribute(type);
                                    imgs[i].removeAttribute(type);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    },

                function ksCallback(json){
                    var documents = json.documents;
                    if(documents.length > 0){
                        dealertempstr += '<ul class=\"ulTxt\">';
                        for(var i = 0;i < documents.length;i++){
                            var item = documents[i];
                            dealertempstr += '<li><a href=\"'+item.url.replace(/https?:/,"")+'\" target=\"_blank\">'+item.title+'</a></li>';
                        }
                        dealertempstr += '</ul>';
                    }
                    if(document.getElementById('dealer0')){
                        document.getElementById('dealer0').innerHTML = dealertempstr;
                    }
                }

                                shtml += '<i><img src="//www1.pcauto.com.cn/2013/price2013/24h.png" title="24小时服务热线"/></i>';

                            }else if(_item.namelistRange == 2){
                                shtml += '<i><img title=\"出售全国\" src="//www1.pcauto.com.cn/2013/price2013/s_sqg.png"/></i>';
                            }
                            shtml += '<i><a href=\"//price.pcauto.com.cn/dealer/commorders/order.jsp?ad=4315&did='+_item.id+'&sgid='+serialGroupId+'\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"icon_price\" title=\"询问商家底价\">询底价</a></i></span></p>';
                            //--------------------
                            shtml += '<p><span class=\"pPicTxt_title\">地址：</span><span class=\"addr\" title=\"'+_item.address+'\">'+cutstr(_item.address,17)+'<a class=\"blue\" href=\"//price.pcauto.com.cn/'+_item.id+'/contact.html\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"地址\">[地图]</a></span></p>';
                            //--------------------
                            if(!!_item.hangNewsName){
                                shtml += '<p><span class=\"pPicTxt_title\">促销：</span><a class=\"sale\" href=\"'+_item.hangNewsUrl.replace(/https?:/,"")+'\" target=\"_blank\" title=\"'+_item.hangNewsName+'\">'+cutstr(_item.hangNewsName,20)+'</a></p>';
                            }else{
                                shtml += '<p>促销：暂无促销</p>';
                            }
                            shtml += '</li>';
                        }
                        shtml += '</ul>';
                    }
                    return shtml;
                }

                function get400Phone(str){
                    var phone = [];
                    phone[0] = str.substr(0,3)+'-'+str.substr(3,3)+'-'+str.substr(6,4);
                    phone[1] = str.substr(11);
                    return phone;
                }

                function getAreaCmsId(id){
                    id =!!(id/1)?(id/1):id;
                    var contains = function(arr, item){
                        for(var i = 0;i<arr.length;i++){
                            if(arr[i] === item){
                                return true;
                            }
                        }
                        return false;
                    };
                    var shenzhen=[4];
                    var beijing=[2,725,257,277,351,354,348,355,353,350,352,137];
                    var shanghai=[3,309,389,382,308,487,157,390,385,305,307,895,310,306,177,302,304,300,402,218,399,299,391,303,587,217];
                    var guangzhou=[1,6,298,533,35,238,288,207,290,463,456,289,459,291,461,288,460,462,464,457,458,432,431,429,435,622,436,433,434,907,438,439,509,599,430,117,545,564,547,550,511,548,584,626,510,546,549,512,197];
                    var chengdu=[87,583,514,423,582,559,422,425,428,328,427,426,538,513,515,424,710,581,77,455,453,452,702,666,604,107,516,580,665,663,664,287];
                    if(contains(shenzhen, id)){
                        return '000049777';
                    }else if(contains(beijing, id)){
                        return '000049772';
                    }else if(contains(shanghai, id)){
                        return '000049222';
                    }else if(contains(guangzhou, id)){
                        return '000048735';
                    }else if(contains(chengdu, id)){
                        return '000049767';
                    }else{
                        return null;
                    }
                }

                function cutstr(str,num){
                    var l = str.replace(/[^\x00-\xff]/gi, "xx").length;
                    if(num < l/2){
                        return str.substr(0, num);
                    }else{
                        return str;
                    }
                }

                }

                function ershouCallback(data){
                    if(!!data){
                        var textBottom = data.textBottom;
                        var html="<div class=\"th\">"
                        html+="<div class=\"mark\">"+serialGroupName+"二手车推荐<\/div>"
                        html+="<\/div>";
                        html+="<div class=\"tb clearfix\">";
                        html+="<ul class=\"esc-list\">";
                        for(var i = 0;i < textBottom.length;i++){
                            var item = textBottom[i];
                            html+="<li>";
                            html+="<a href=\""+item.linkurl.replace(/https?:/,"")+"\" target=\"_blank\" onclick=\"countEscPv();\">";
                            html+="<img width=\"135\" height=\"100\" alt=\"\" src=\""+item.thumbpictureurl.replace(/https?:/,"")+"\">";
                            html+="<span class=\"esc-name\">"+item.description+"<\/span>";
                            html+="</a>";
                            html+="<p class=\"esc-des\">";
                            html+="<span class=\"esc-price\">"+item.price+"<\/span>";
                            html+="<span class=\"esc-km\">"+item.distance+"<\/span>";
                            html+="<\/p>";
                            html+="<\/li>";
                        }
                        html+="<\/ul>";
                        html+="<\/div>";
                        $("#esc-div").html(html);
                    }
                }

        <script type="text/javascript">
            window.onload=function(){
                var tl_btn = $("#JtabClubTl .pagination .toc");
                var tl_img = $("#JtabClubTl .contentdiv");
                var clubTimmer=null;
                function clubTlChang(index){
                    tl_img.eq(index).show().siblings().hide();
                    tl_btn.eq(index).addClass("current").siblings().removeClass("current");
                }
                function clubTlPlay(){
                    var f_index = tl_btn.index($('#JtabClubTl .pagination').find(".current"));
                    clubTlChang(((f_index+1)%3));
                }
                tl_btn.mouseover(function(){
                    clearInterval(clubTimmer);
                    var f_index = tl_btn.index(this);
                    clubTlChang(f_index);
                });
                tl_btn.mouseout(function(){
                    clubTimmer = setInterval(clubTlPlay,4000)
                });

                clubTlChang(0);
                clubTimmer = setInterval(clubTlPlay,4000)
            }
        </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            (function(){
                var scrollFixed = function(id){
                    var fix = document.getElementById(id);
                    if(!fix) return;
                    var box = fix.parentNode;
                    box.style.height = box.offsetHeight+"px";
                    var top = getElemTop(fix);
                    ret();
                    addEvent(window,"scroll",function(){
                        ret()
                    });

                    function ret(){
                        var scrollTop = getScrollTop();

                        if(scrollTop >= top){
                            addClass(box,"nav-scrollFixed")
                        }else{
                            removeClass(box,"nav-scrollFixed")
                        }
                    }

                }
                //去除字符两边空格
                String.prototype.trim = function(){
                    return this.replace(/(^\s*)|(\s*$)/g,"")
                }

                function removeClass(elem,className){
                    var oldClass = elem.className,
                    reg = new RegExp(className+"\\b\\s?","g");

                    newClass = oldClass.replace(reg,"").trim();
                    elem.className = newClass;
                    return newClass;
                }

                function addClass(elem,className){
                    var old = removeClass(elem,className);
                    elem.className = old+" "+className;
                }

                function getScrollTop(){
                    return document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop;
                }

                function addEvent(elem,type,fn){
                    if(elem.addEventListener){
                        elem.addEventListener(type, fn, false)
                    }else{
                        elem.attachEvent("on"+type, fn)
                    }
                }

                function getElemTop(element){
                    var top = element.offsetTop;

                    var current = element.offsetParent;

                    while(current){

                        top += current.offsetTop;
                        current = current.offsetParent;

                    }

                    return top;

                }

                window.scrollFixed = scrollFixed;

            })(window);

            scrollFixed("Jheader");

                    });
                }

            });

                  <script type="text/javascript">
                    // 帖子图片缩放
                    $("#topic_list .img img").load(function() {
                        var $width = 120;
                        var $height = 80;
                        var pic = this;
                        if (pic.width >= $width && pic.height >= $height) {
                            var imgheight;
                            var imgwidth;
                            if (pic.width / pic.height > $width / $height) {
                                imgheight = pic.height = $height;
                                imgwidth = pic.width;
                            } else {
                                imgwidth = pic.width = $width;
                                imgheight = pic.height;
                            }
                            if (imgwidth == $width) {
                                pic.style.top = ($height - imgheight) / 2 + "px";
                            } else if (imgheight == $height) {
                                pic.style.left = ($width - imgwidth) / 2 + "px";
                            }
                            $(pic).parent().hide().addClass("show").fadeIn();
                        } else {
                            $(pic).parent().hide();
                        }
                    });

                    $("#topic_list .img img").filter("[src2]").each(function(){
                        var loadimg = $(this).attr("src2");
                        var index = loadimg.indexOf("/bbs6/");
                        if (index != -1) {
                            var year = loadimg.substring(index+6, index+6+4);
                            if (year*1 <= 1212) {
                                loadimg = loadimg.replace("_120x80", "_1024x1024");
                            }
                        }
                        $(this).attr("src", loadimg);
                    });
                </script>

        <!-- 支付宝询价 start-->
        <script type="text/javascript">
        var domainUrl = '//price.pcauto.com.cn';
        var mUrl = '//m.pcauto.com.cn';
        // PC线上域名：//price.pcauto.com.cn
        var autoPirceToken;
        //申请令牌
        $(function(){
            $.ajax({
                url: domainUrl + '/interface/token/applyToken.jsp?_t=' + new Date().getTime(),
                type: 'GET',
                dataType: 'jsonp',
                success: function (rs) {
                    autoPirceToken = rs.token;
                }
            })
        });
        //显示二维码
        function showPop(channelId) {
            var url = getSrc(channelId);
            if(!Boolean(url)) return;
            $("#alipay_qrcode").attr("src", url);
            if(channelId==1125){
            	 payClick(channelId);
            }
           
            if(curCityId <= 0 || curCityId == 217){
                return;
            }else{
                $("#JbgMarkPay").removeClass("hide");
                $("#Jpop-zfb").removeClass("hide");
                $("#JbgMarkPay").show();
                $("#Jpop-zfb").show();
            }
        }
        //生成二维码路径
        function getSrc(channelId){
            var sgid = "4580"; //车系id
            var mid = "";//车型id
            var did = '';
            var token = autoPirceToken;
            var rid = curCityId;
            if (! (sgid > 0 || mid > 0)) {
                return null;
            }
            var referrer = document.referrer;
            if (referrer == '') {
                referrer = window.location.href;
                refererType = 2;
            }
            if (referrer.indexOf("?") != -1 || referrer.indexOf("#") != -1) {
            var str1 = "";
            var ipos = 0;
            if (referrer.indexOf("?") != -1) {
                ipos = referrer.indexOf("?");
                str1 = referrer.substring(0, ipos); //取前部分
                referrer = str1 + "?alipay=1";
            } else if (referrer.indexOf("#") != -1) {
                ipos = referrer.indexOf("#");
                str1 = referrer.substring(0, ipos); //取前部分
                referrer = str1 + "?alipay=1";
            }
            } else {
                referrer = referrer + "?alipay=1";
            }
            var refererType = 1;
            if (referrer == '') {
                referrer = window.location.href;
                refererType = 2;
            }
            var cookie = getCookieMes('pcsuv');
            var payType = 0; //是否全款购车，0：是，1：否
            var protocolStr = document.location.protocol;
            var loanCarFlagWap = 0; //选择贷款购车，不给用户发短信。是否选择贷款购车，1：是，0：否。
            
         
            var post_url = protocolStr + mUrl + "/wap_dazzle/index/_do_order_proxy.jsp?reqResource=wapOrder2013&domainName=DealerCommOrder&serialGroupId=" + sgid
            + "&modelId=" + mid
            + "&dealerId=" + did
            + "&regionId=" + rid
            + "&wap=1&referer=" + encodeURIComponent(referrer)
            + "&refererType=" + refererType
            + "&origin=1&isAward=1&payType=0"
            + "&cookie=" + cookie
            + "&html_TOKEN=" + token
            + "&loanCarFlagWap=0" + "&orderPortal=";
            var adId = 12506;
            if(channelId==1125){
            	adId = 12483;
              }
               
            var redirect_url = protocolStr + mUrl + "/wap_dazzle/2_0/ask_success_zfb.jsp?ad="+ adId 
            + "&modelId=" + mid
            + "&regionId=" + rid 
            + "&serialGroupId=" + sgid;
            var transferUrl = protocolStr + mUrl + "/wap_dazzle/interface/transfer_page_for_ask.jsp?post_url=" + encodeURIComponent(post_url)
            + "&redirect_url=" + encodeURIComponent(redirect_url);
            var logo = protocolStr +"//www1.pcauto.com.cn/zt/gz2018072317/zfb/icon.png";
            var url = protocolStr + domainUrl + "/dealer/interface/qrcode/action/generate_qr_code_v2.jsp?url=" + encodeURIComponent(transferUrl) + "&logo=" + logo;
            return url;
        }
        //自定义事件
        function payClick(channelId){
            var img = new Image;
            img.src = "//count.pcauto.com.cn/count.php?channel="+channelId+"&screen=" + screen.width + "*" + screen.height + "&refer=" + encodeURIComponent(document.referrer) + "&anticache=" + new Date().getTime() + "&url=" + encodeURIComponent(location.href) + "&from=event";
        }
        function getCookieMes(name){
            return document.cookie.replace(new RegExp(".*(?:^|; )" + name + "=([^;]*).*|.*"), "$1");
        }
        //隐藏二维码
        function hidePop(){
            $("#JbgMarkPay").hide();
            $("#Jpop-zfb").hide();
        }
        </script>
